# <a name="microsoft-365-encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="0e41b-103">Microsoft 365 加密鏈</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0e41b-103">Microsoft 365 encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0e41b-104">Microsoft 365 會利用許多不同的憑證提供者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0e41b-104">Microsoft 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0e41b-105">下列說明當存取 Microsoft 365 時，客戶可能會遇到的已知 Microsoft 365 根憑證的完整清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0e41b-105">The following describes the complete list of known Microsoft 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Microsoft 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0e41b-106">如需您可能需要在自己的基礎結構中安裝之憑證的詳細資訊，請參閱[Plan for 協力廠商 SSL 憑證以取得 Microsoft 365](../enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0e41b-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](../enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0e41b-107">下列憑證資訊適用于 Microsoft 365 的所有全球和國內雲端實例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0e41b-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Microsoft 365.</span></span>
